          <div class="breakout-section-box">
           <h2 class="close-heading custom-h5">
            You are a part of the
            <div class="thin custom-h1">
             Pacific Flyway
            </div>
           </h2>
           <p>
            Each year more than a billion birds migrate along the Pacific Flyway, which stretches from the North Slope of Alaska to Central and South America.
           </p>
           <br/>
           <div class="editorial-card dark no-border">
            <div class="editorial-card-content">
             <h3 class="editorial-card-title blue custom-h4">
              <a href="/flyways">
               About the Flyways
              </a>
             </h3>
             <p>
             </p>
             <p>
              Audubon follows the birds to our work, organizing our conservation strategies along the four flyways of the Americas.
             </p>

     <div class="flyway-section flyway-section-2">
      <div class="breakout-section no-hero contextual-links-region" data-background="https://nas-national-prod.s3.amazonaws.com/styles/get_outside/s3/grafton-miss-image-cropped.png?itok=R-2x-o3k" style="background-image: none; background-color: #444444;">
       <div class="breakout-section-content light-text">
        <div class="row space-top space-bottom double">
         <div class="columns large-4">
          <div class="breakout-section-box">
           <h2 class="close-heading custom-h5">
            You are a part of the
            <div class="thin custom-h1">
             Mississippi Flyway
            </div>
           </h2>
           <p>
            The Mississippi Flyway is named for the great river underpinning the migration route followed by 60 percent of North America's birds, including the American White Pelicans, Least Terns, and Prothonotary Warblers. By restoring habitat from the headwaters of the Mississippi to the Louisiana Delta, Audubon is protecting birds year-round.
           </p>
           <br/>
           <div class="editorial-card dark no-border">
            <div class="editorial-card-content">

              Audubon follows the birds to our work, organizing our conservation strategies along the four flyways of the Americas.

     <div class="flyway-section flyway-section-3">
      <div class="breakout-section no-hero contextual-links-region" data-background="https://nas-national-prod.s3.amazonaws.com/styles/get_outside/s3/flyaway/background/_MG_9657_Atlantic_JohnHuba.jpg?itok=cG_jVTtY" style="background-image: none; background-color: #444444;">
       <div class="breakout-section-content light-text">
        <div class="row space-top space-bottom double">
         <div class="columns large-4">
          <div class="breakout-section-box">
           <h2 class="close-heading custom-h5">
            You are a part of the
            <div class="thin custom-h1">
             Atlantic Flyway
            </div>
           </h2>
           <p>
            From the forests of New England, where birds like the Wood Thrush nest and breed, to the beaches and marshlands that stretch down the coast and provide habitat for Piping Plovers and Saltmarsh Sparrows, Audubon is employing tactics as diverse as this flyway's ecosystems to protect the millions of birds that depend on this flyway.
           </p>
           <br/>
           <div class="editorial-card dark no-border">

              Audubon follows the birds to our work, organizing our conservation strategies along the four flyways of the Americas.
             </p>

             The time associated with your ticket purchase is your ENTRY time.

     <div class="flyway-section flyway-section-4">
      <div class="breakout-section no-hero contextual-links-region" data-background="https://nas-national-prod.s3.amazonaws.com/styles/get_outside/s3/mallard_motel.jpg?itok=fmjhr_XC" style="background-image: none; background-color: #444444;">
       <div class="breakout-section-content light-text">
        <div class="row space-top space-bottom double">
         <div class="columns large-4">
          <div class="breakout-section-box">
           <h2 class="close-heading custom-h5">
            You are a part of the
            <div class="thin custom-h1">
             Central Flyway
            </div>
           </h2>
           <p>
            Stretching from the Rocky Mountains to the Great Plains to the desert Southwest and the western Gulf Coast, the Central Flyway comprises more than half of the continental U.S.'s land mass and includes 509 Important Bird Areas. Across this expansive flyway, such iconic bird species as the Greater Sage Grouse, Sandhill Crane, and Yellow-billed Cuckoo drive Audubon's work to protect threatened ecosystems.
           </p>
           <br/>
           <div class="editorial-card dark no-border">
            <div class="editorial-card-content">
             <h3 class="editorial-card-title blue custom-h4">
              <a href="/flyways">
               About the Flyways
              </a>
             </h3>
             <p>
             </p>
             <p>
              Audubon follows the birds to our work, organizing our conservation strategies along the four flyways of the Americas.
             </p>
             <br/>
             <a class="editorial-card-link" href="/flyways" title="Learn More About the Flyways">
              Learn More About the Flyways
             </a>
            </div>
